He ensured my partner and I were picked up at Yangshuo Railway Station, knowing that it would be difficult to get a Didi during the holiday period. Jason also arranged transportation for us throughout our stay in Yangshuo so we could visit all the hotspots. Jason‚Äôs proactivity ranks amongst the best customer service I‚Äôve seen in a hotel anywhere in the world. 

The location of the hotel is fantastic, allowing for easy access to key hotspots in Yangshuo. The hotel is also very adept at arranging transportation if needed. The hotel is close to spots like Moon Hill Mountain and West Street - key tourist hotspots in Yangshuo. 

The food at the hotel is absolutely exquisite and also priced very economically. We were blown away by the quality of the food and the fresh ingredients used. I would highly recommend the hotel food. In addition, the hotel serves free snacks at lunch and also gives a free night time snack every day of your stay! I should also add you can pay using a Visa card at this hotel. This was a notable perk for us as foreigners. 

The rooms are fantastic, with amazing views of the beautiful unique Yangshuo mountains. The beds are huge in size and the bathtub is a dream! Very clean and well maintained rooms. The hotel is also extremely clean which is critical for me when reviewing hotels - this hotel does not disappoint in the hygiene department! 

I want to finish off by again praising the brilliant customer service and attention given to customers. We will definitely come back to this hotel in the future and highly recommend this hotel as a first class choice in Yangshuo.

msg:The hotel is located right in the middle of the two core areas of Yangshuo. On one side is the county town (West Street, Eternal Love, Impression of Liu Sanjie), and on the other side is Yulong River, Ruyi Peak, and Shili Gallery (just a road). Sometimes you need to take a taxi, and sometimes you rent an electric car, which is very convenient. (Local roads are winding and narrow, so you need to pay attention to safety when riding an electric car) The hotel provides some vehicle pick-up and drop-off services, which is great. The hotel's hardware facilities are good, and the room part is not inferior to a five-star hotel. The scenery and environment around the hotel are also good, quiet and elegant. The hotel staff is enthusiastic and enthusiastic, which makes people happy. Disadvantages: 1. The signal of the TV remote control panel interferes with the air-conditioning panel, and the air-conditioning panel will make a beeping sound when pressing the remote control. 2. The hotel assists in booking performance tickets, and the price discount is not large, and the seat position may not be the best (the local performance ticket channels and prices have formed an industry black box operation, which is very weird, and the hotel probably tried its best). "Eternal Love" can choose a seat in the front of Area A. The middle part of B1 (or the back row of B2) in "Impression of Liu Sanjie" is very good, which is similar to the so-called presidential seat in Area A. 3. Compared with the room rate of more than 700 yuan, the breakfast is simpler and tastes average. Overall, I am very satisfied with my stay.

If you are a young man who is looking for excitement and wants to eat, drink, have fun and play disco, it is convenient to live in West Street.
